# Commit 733d99ab74

**Date:** 2026-03-05T21:28  
**Author:** Michael Schürig <michael@schuerig.de>

## Commit message

Rename Comparison to PitchComparison across entire codebase

Achieve naming symmetry with the PitchMatching* family by renaming all
Comparison* types to PitchComparison* and PitchDiscriminationProfile to
PitchComparisonProfile. Pure rename refactoring with no functional changes.

Source (~30 files): renamed types, protocols, methods, properties, enum
cases, directory Comparison/ → PitchComparison/, CSV format value
"comparison" → "pitchComparison".

Tests (~35 files): renamed all references, mocks, helpers, assertions.

Docs (~19 files): updated project-context, architecture, glossary, PRD,
epics, UX spec, arc42 docs, sprint-status, README.

Co-Authored-By: Claude Opus 4.6 <noreply@anthropic.com>

Let me look at the problem differently. The test `refreshExportWithRecords` creates a service, saves a record, calls `refreshExport()`, and expects `exportCSV != nil`. The `refreshExport` catches errors silently and sets `exportCSV = nil`. Perhaps the fetch is throwing. Let me check if maybe `PitchComparisonRecord.self` in the `ModelContainer` init is wrong:

Actually, I bet the issue is that `TrainingDataExporter.export(from:)` returns `CSVExportSchema.headerRow` when no records are found, and the comparison `csv == CSVExportSchema.headerRow` sets `exportCSV = nil`. If `fetchAllPitchComparisons()` returns empty despite saving, that would cause the test to fail.

Let me check if maybe the test is using a different `ModelContext` for saving vs fetching. Looking at `makeService()`:

```swift
let container = try makeTestContainer()
let context = ModelContext(container)
let dataStore = TrainingDataStore(modelContext: context)
```

And then `try dataStore.save(makeComparison())` inserts + saves into that context. Then `service.refreshExport()` uses the same `dataStore` which uses the same context. Should work.

Maybe the issue is that `@Observable` state changes aren't working in a test context. `exportCSV` is a `private(set) var` in an `@Observable` class. Let me check if `service.exportCSV` is accessible. Actually, this is a read of a property, should work fine.
